Test t9485: DLL resource library for 32bit Windows links RSRC resource file


Description
Test creates resource-only 32bit DLL file from resource file ../objlib/euroasm.res.
Resource file was compiled by Microsoft Resource Compiler in subfolder objlib from the script euroasm.rc 
LANGUAGE LANG_NEUTRAL, SUBLANG_NEUTRAL
EASM ICON "easm.ico"
EUROASM ICON "euroasm.ico"
VITSOFT ICON "vitsoft.ico"
with command rc.exe euroasm.rc
See also
LinkerCombinations  
Tested procedures
PfdllCompile   PfrsrcLoadPgm
